<h2 class="kt-adv-heading81208_eaf098-d0 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading81208_eaf098-d0">Meet Clara Mae</h2>



<p>Hello there! My name is <strong>Clara Mae Whitmore</strong>, and I’m a pastry chef from the charming city of Charleston, South Carolina — where the scent of vanilla, butter, and warm biscuits fills the air and every bake tells a story.</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-advancedbtn kb-buttons-wrap kb-btns81208_3d66ba-39"><a class="kb-button kt-button button kb-btn81208_af2500-72 kt-btn-size-standard kt-btn-width-type-auto kb-btn-global-inherit  kt-btn-has-text-true kt-btn-has-svg-true  wp-block-button__link more-button wp-block-kadence-singlebtn" href="https://bakedtales.com/about-us/"><span class="kt-btn-inner-text">About  <strong>Clara </strong></span><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRightCircle kt-btn-icon-side-right"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 16 16 12 12 8"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"/></svg></span></a></div>
